\DoxyCodeLine{00182\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{eigen_2Eigen_2src_2Core_2util_2Macros_8h_a9efec3cfd22b9a33bead9c6718d128da}{EIGEN\_DEVICE\_FUNC}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00183\ \ \ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ Scalar\ \mbox{\hyperlink{structEigen_1_1internal_1_1digamma__impl_a55a556100db7911f893d5898b345a953}{run}}(Scalar\ x)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00184\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00185\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00186\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ Psi\ (digamma)\ function\ (modified\ for\ Eigen)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00187\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00188\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00189\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ SYNOPSIS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00190\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00191\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ double\ x,\ y,\ psi();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00192\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00193\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ y\ =\ psi(\ x\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00194\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00195\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00196\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00197\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00198\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ d\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00199\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ psi(x)\ \ =\ \ -\/-\/\ ln\ |\ (x)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00200\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ dx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00201\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00202\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ is\ the\ logarithmic\ derivative\ of\ the\ gamma\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00203\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ For\ integer\ x,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00204\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ n-\/1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00205\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00206\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ psi(n)\ =\ -\/EUL\ \ +\ \ \ >\ \ 1/k.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00207\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00208\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ k=1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ If\ x\ is\ negative,\ it\ is\ transformed\ to\ a\ positive\ argument\ by\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ reflection\ formula\ \ psi(1-\/x)\ =\ psi(x)\ +\ pi\ cot(pi\ x).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00212\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ For\ general\ positive\ x,\ the\ argument\ is\ made\ greater\ than\ 10}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ using\ the\ recurrence\ \ psi(x+1)\ =\ psi(x)\ +\ 1/x.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ Then\ the\ following\ asymptotic\ expansion\ is\ applied:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00434\ \textcolor{comment}{*\ Implementation\ of\ ndtri.\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00436\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00437\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Inverse\ of\ Normal\ distribution\ function\ (modified\ for\ Eigen).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00438\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00439\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00440\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ SYNOPSIS:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00441\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00442\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ double\ x,\ y,\ ndtri();}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00443\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00444\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ x\ =\ ndtri(\ y\ );}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00445\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00446\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00447\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00448\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00449\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00450\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Returns\ the\ argument,\ x,\ for\ which\ the\ area\ under\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00451\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Gaussian\ probability\ density\ function\ (integrated\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00452\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ minus\ infinity\ to\ x)\ is\ equal\ to\ y.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00453\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00454\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00455\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ small\ arguments\ 0\ <\ y\ <\ exp(-\/2),\ the\ program\ computes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00456\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ z\ =\ sqrt(\ -\/2.0\ *\ log(y)\ );\ \ then\ the\ approximation\ is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00457\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ x\ =\ z\ -\/\ log(z)/z\ \ -\/\ (1/z)\ P(1/z)\ /\ Q(1/z).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00458\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ are\ two\ rational\ functions\ P/Q,\ one\ for\ 0\ <\ y\ <\ exp(-\/32)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and\ the\ other\ for\ y\ up\ to\ exp(-\/2).\ \ For\ larger\ arguments,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ w\ =\ y\ -\/\ 0.5,\ and\ \ x/sqrt(2pi)\ =\ w\ +\ w**3\ R(w**2)/S(w**2)).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ACCURACY:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ Relative\ error:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00466\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ arithmetic\ \ \ domain\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \#\ trials\ \ \ \ \ \ peak\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ rms}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ DEC\ \ \ \ \ \ 0.125,\ 1\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 5500\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 9.5e-\/17\ \ \ \ \ 2.1e-\/17}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ DEC\ \ \ \ \ \ 6e-\/39,\ 0.135\ \ \ \ \ 3500\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 5.7e-\/17\ \ \ \ \ 1.3e-\/17}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00469\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ IEEE\ \ \ \ \ 0.125,\ 1\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 20000\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 7.2e-\/16\ \ \ \ \ 1.3e-\/16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00470\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ IEEE\ \ \ \ \ 3e-\/308,\ 0.135\ \ \ 50000\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 4.6e-\/16\ \ \ \ \ 9.8e-\/17}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00471\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ERROR\ MESSAGES:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00474\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00475\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ message\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ condition\ \ \ \ value\ returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00476\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ndtri\ domain\ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\ <=\ 0\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ -\/MAXNUM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00477\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ndtri\ domain\ \ \ \ \ \ \ x\ >=\ 1\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ MAXNUM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00478\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00479\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00480\ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00481\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Cephes\ Math\ Library\ Release\ 2.2:\ June,\ 1992}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00482\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Copyright\ 1985,\ 1987,\ 1992\ by\ Stephen\ L.\ Moshier}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00483\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ Direct\ inquiries\ to\ 30\ Frost\ Street,\ Cambridge,\ MA\ 02140}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00484\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01208\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Derivative\ of\ a\ Gamma\ random\ variable\ sample\ with\ respect\ to\ alpha.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01209\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01210\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ Consider\ a\ sample\ of\ a\ Gamma\ random\ variable\ with\ the\ concentration}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01211\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ parameter\ alpha:\ sample\ \string~\ Gamma(alpha,\ 1).\ The\ reparameterization}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01212\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ derivative\ that\ we\ want\ to\ compute\ is\ dsample\ /\ dalpha\ =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01213\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ d\ igammainv(alpha,\ u)\ /\ dalpha,\ where\ u\ =\ igamma(alpha,\ sample).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01214\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ However,\ this\ formula\ is\ numerically\ unstable\ and\ expensive,\ so\ instead}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01215\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ we\ use\ implicit\ differentiation:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01216\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01217\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ igamma(alpha,\ sample)\ =\ u,\ where\ u\ \string~\ Uniform(0,\ 1).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01218\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ Apply\ d\ /\ dalpha\ to\ both\ sides:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01219\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ d\ igamma(alpha,\ sample)\ /\ dalpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01220\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ +\ d\ igamma(alpha,\ sample)\ /\ dsample\ *\ dsample/dalpha\ \ =\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01221\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ d\ igamma(alpha,\ sample)\ /\ dalpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01222\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ +\ Gamma(sample\ |\ alpha,\ 1)\ dsample\ /\ dalpha\ =\ 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01223\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ dsample/dalpha\ =\ -\/\ (d\ igamma(alpha,\ sample)\ /\ dalpha)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01224\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ /\ Gamma(sample\ |\ alpha,\ 1)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01225\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01226\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ Here\ Gamma(sample\ |\ alpha,\ 1)\ is\ the\ PDF\ of\ the\ Gamma\ distribution}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01227\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ (note\ that\ the\ derivative\ of\ the\ CDF\ w.r.t.\ sample\ is\ the\ PDF).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01228\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ See\ the\ reference\ below\ for\ more\ details.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01229\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01230\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ The\ derivative\ of\ igamma(alpha,\ sample)\ is\ computed\ by\ forward}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01231\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ differentiation\ of\ the\ igamma\ code.\ Division\ by\ the\ Gamma\ PDF\ is\ performed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01232\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ in\ the\ same\ code,\ increasing\ the\ accuracy\ and\ speed\ due\ to\ cancellation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01233\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ of\ some\ terms.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01234\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01235\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ *\ Accuracy\ estimation.\ For\ each\ alpha\ in\ [10\string^-\/2,\ 10\string^-\/1...10\string^3]\ we\ sample}}
